The reality is in America and in most of the world, if you're cut off from the banking system, it makes it incredibly difficult to do almost anything, much less uh you know, you can't even pay your mortgage system. And it's even worse if you're a big business like Only Fans. And they were getting backed into a corner. On August 19th, 2021, they did something pretty crazy. They announced that in October 1st, they would no longer allow adultoriented content to exist on Only Fans. And by this point, like that was the name of the business. That's what the whole business is, is an adult website. They were suddenly saying, "Hey, Only Fans, we're not going to allow any more of that going forward." Stokeley, who was still involved in leading the business, he basically went on media tours and said, "Hey, the banks have forced us to do this. We can't be in the adult business anymore. Creators went and started to look up on other sites like one's called Fansley and stuff like that. Also, never seen that one." Uh, but but in the end, like Tim and his folks said, the reason we have to do this is we have to be connected to the money system to be a business. And here was Only Fans unable to do that. But in a crazy turn of events, 6 days later, Only Fans came out and said, "Well, we're reversing that decision." Suddenly, they had managed to find new banking partners. What had happened in the background was creators and the public had started to pressure the banks. Tim going out and being public about the banks causing the shutdown of adult content had caused all those people who were on both sides of those transactions to put pressures on those banks. In reality, there had been kind of a standoff. Also, those banks, they want to make money. And the way they make money is by having money flow through their system. And here was a big source of that money about to be totally cut off. The reality is all of these kind of shadow industries, ammo, guns, adult content, cannabis, they all exist in kind of a gray area and there's an inherent tension there. The banks and all the financial system, they want to be making money from those transactions. There's a lot of cash there. At the same time, they're getting pressure from the other side, which is like gray area is gray area for a reason. Uh it's sometimes outside the law, and sometimes there's a lot of people in those industries doing not good stuff. And the interesting thing of where America's gone, uh so much of our regulation and expectation about the morality of society is getting not done by the government or by the courts or by the laws or by legislators. It's getting done by the whims and decisions being made by big corporations. And it's kind of crazy if you look at it now. It's become a normal expectation that we expect all these folks who are running businesses to become both the morality and legal police for the American society. Stokeley had had enough. 4 months later he stepped down in December 2021. There was a new CEO for a bit and then in 2023 they brought in a new CEO to run the company. That person well is a lawyer. That person's name is Key Blair and that tells you what's going to be the real battles for Only Fans going forward. Over the next four years, Radvinsky ran the company his way. It was totally out of the way. The company had one mission, and that was to put money in the pocket of Radvinsky. Over the next four years, the company has distributed $1.4 billion in cash to this one man alone. Even after all that distribution, the company was making $46 million per employee. But that's not the biggest problem happening. The biggest disruption coming at this next point into 2022 and beyond is AI.
